He even gave me a Veterans discount. Over the past 4 years we have stayed in touch via Facebook, sharing photos and being a member of his customer community. It truly is a community‚Ä¶ Once you are a member you are one for life. That says a lot to me about the business that is being run here. I am not an expert at all, but I do know this is a business you can trust and will always be there for you. If I sent him a message right now, 4 years later I would get a quick and professional response and not the typical "hey do you want to buy" something. < Text>
We have gotten two rescue dogs through One Of a Kind Bulldogs and have been so impressed! It just so happened that each dog came to us as a second placement after living in homes where they were loved by their humans, but a second dog in the home was becoming increasingly aggressive toward them over time. Of course, only a breeder who truly cares about his dogs would do all of the leg work (pun intended) to find these dogs their fur-ever homes.

The One of a Kind Bulldogs foster volunteer that we have worked with both times has been AMAZING. Trish has such a heart for and natural intuition for matching dogs and people, and of course, a heart for placing dogs in homes that would otherwise be euthanized.

But don't just listen to a human review--what would the dogs say? Well, this week I took advantage of the kenneling service that One of a Kind Bulldogs offers its customers, and it was so neat to bring our dog back to where she came from. I watched her perk up in the car as we got closer, get out of the car and walk right up to the gate, tail wiggling. The owner Ary came out, bent down and lovingly kissed her on the head, and took her off her leash. She looked at me inquisitively, but followed Ary right inside--no collar required. Wow! This is no puppy mill!

I am so impressed with One of a Kind Bulldogs and am excited to refer all of my bulldog-loving friends to them!</Text>

<username>bfloss88< /username><Time>1473991322668<//Time><Rating>5<//Rating><text>As the title suggests One of a Kind Bulldogs is truly a one of a kind experience with a one of a kind owner with One of a Kind dogs and a One of a Kind family.

Brace yourself this will be long but if you are serious about finding a beautiful dog and a great experience you'll read.

After losing my last bulldog it took me some time to get another.  After being burned by a few other places, including by the owners of my last, I stumbled upon One of a Kind Bulldogs.

The first thing I noticed in their message was the work, compassion and commitment to all animals especially bulldogs.  I decided to reach out and after talking for a while I was sold.  The whole experience was nothing short amazing.  We worked out the details, which involved getting my dog 1,500 miles to me. A week and a half later I had the most amazing little girl ever.

What I wasn't expecting was the family I would be getting with her.  Ary has set up a network with all of his bulldog families to share photos, ask advice, and get to know one another.  Bulldogs are not an easy breed and it is really nice to have a place to turn with so many experienced owners. I have developed many lasting friendships with many of the other families. It is fun getting to know each other and our beautiful dogs.

Not only is One of a Kind a great place, you are getting the highest quality Old English Bulldog with the highest level of care.  You dont get any of the health issues you get from standard English Bulldogs (I know first hand I've had both).  You get healthy, strong, and amazing Old English Bulldogs.  Its fun to see people's reactions to a bulldog at the top of the trail.  My girl goes on hikes, love to swim, and loves the outdoors. You won't get that with other bulldogs.  But she still has the goofy and lazy moments that make bulldogs so great.

If you question the integrity of One of a Kind Bulldogs take it from me give them a call.  You will see the passionate through their rescue/rehab and breeding work, you will see commitment in their healthy beautiful dogs, and you will see the integrity once you step foot in their world.

You wont be disappointed, I'm not and I guarantee the rest of the One of a Kind family isn't.<//text>< Pictures>

<text>We came across this breeder when researching bulldog puppies, and contacted him to book an appointment to visit.  Ary took the time to ask us plenty of questions to determine if this breed would be a good fit in our lives, with our current dog and living situation.  I truly felt like he cared about who would be taking his puppies, rather than just trying to sell them to just anyone.  Once he realized we were a good fit, he advised us of the sex of the dog he would recommend to get along best with our other dog, and invited us to come visit the same morning.  The kennels are huge, clean, and have plenty of toys to play with, including pools to splash around in. We got to meet the older dogs, including some that he had rescued, and we got to see the puppies. Since adopting our girl in January, I've contacted him day and night with questions, and he's always answered within moments.  We recently boarded our girl with him while we were on vacation for almost 3 weeks, and he sent us video updates. <user_id>112739588008524524733< /user_id>< Review>
So I had a flat tire on a Sunday morning. I went to a coffee shop and furiously researched new tire options. Both my first (Continental Pro Contact EcoPlus) and second choice (Firestone Precision Touring) were on backorder on TireRack, so I decided to call around local tire shops. When I got Mission Tires on the phone on Sunday noon, a gentleman named Gil assured me he could get a four-pack of the Continental by Monday 11am and get me my car back by Monday night. I was skeptical because the Continental seemed to be on backorder in various places, not just TireRack, so I pointed that out to him, but he checked his system and insisted that he could get them Monday morning. Long story short: three days, >100 miles on the freeway with a spare tire, three apologetic phone calls, and a promise of an additional discount later, I finally drove into Mission Tire's garage on Thursday(!) afternoon to have the new tires installed. Conveniently Gil was not in on Thursday, and no one knew about any discount that I was supposed to receive as an apology. Oh well. When they handed me back the keys two hours later and said thank you, LUCKILY I decided to walk around the car and inspect the tires. One of the four was still an old tire ‚Äî they had forgotten to change the fourth tire! 30 minutes later, with the fourth tire installed, Mission Tire's and my ways parted forever.

I understand the tire business is very competetive, not least thanks to TireRack & co., but promising availability just to get my business without actually knowing what the availability is, is unacceptable. And please get your act together and use checklists to make sure you don't let your customers drive off the lot with only three tires replaced. It's not rocket science.< /Review>

< text>
Separate off-leash areas for big and small dogs set up within the new West Hollywood Park, right next to basketball courts. Artificial K9 turf is safe for dogs and makes for a green looking park that stays green. Benches, water stations and trees make this a nice spot to spend time in and a super fun place for dogs to run around and play.

Note that large dog park is closed on Wednesdays from 9-10am and small dog park is closed on Wednesdays from 10-11am for maintenance.</text>

<Review>Two separate closures divided by the basketball court; one for small dogs, one for medium & large dogs. There is a good amount of space for the dogs to play along with tennis balls and water fountains in both closures. For the most part, people do a decent job of cleaning up after their dogs, which is nice and crucial for repeat visits. Plenty of seating area for the owners to kick back. The only drawback is some of the regular owners who are a bit overprotective and stand-offish with some of the other dogs/owners. But that's not the fault of the space. Good parking a stone's throw away at the WeHo library parking structure, with the first hour or two free with validation at the park manager's window by the playground.< /Review><pictures>None< /pictures><resp>None< /resp>< Gmap_id>

<Text>This may be the best casual restaurant on the waterfront in downtown San Diego. The Beach Hut has all the bases covered: Delicious food, excellent cordial service, comfy atmosphere and prime location.

The sandwiches and coffee are superb. My "Stay Classy" breakfast burrito with sausage, cheddar, avocado eggs etc was super tasty, hearty, hot and filling on a nice breezy morning. I also really like their "Skinny Dipper"(roast beef, cheddar, onions veges au jus). And the big chocolate chip cookies are yummy.

Their Ryan Bros coffee is outstanding and at .50 cent refills an excellent value.

I have been watching the World Cup there(big screens on walls as well as large ones in booths for prime viewing) which has been alot of fun.

Service by manager Brittany and Crew is really outstanding..ranks in my top 10 in San Diego and they really know how to make really amazing sandwiches.

The location is unbeatable facing the water/USS Midway Museum with a nice outdoor lounge to soak up the rays.<//Text></record>

<review>Desperate to find parking to go whale-watching, we ended up parking at the Marriott (here's a tip - if you're here for longer than 3 hours, like we were, then park at the Amtrak station, it's only $17.  We ended up paying $25 at the Marriott!) - and on the way to the whalewatching, we wanted a sandwich and it being Christmas day - almost NOTHING was open.  we walked past Beach Hut Deli, my husband said hey, it's convenient, let's try it - I figured it would be small portions, probably not very good, and way overpriced - I mean, it had to be - as it was in such a high touristy  spot.  BOY was I wrong!  I can honestly say, they were about the best sandwiches we've EVER had.  My husband had (I think) turkey/avocado/pickle, blue cheese, tomato (toasted) on wheat bread - and you think - well, it's just a sandwich, how good can it be?  IT WAS UNBELIEVABLE!  Normally (at least in florida), you'd get a smear of avocado, so small you'd have to dig around to find it - not here - there were HUGE slices of avocado - all the way through the sandwich - sandwich was fresh, crunchy, DELICIOUS - I honestly can't speak highly enough about the sandwich.  Silly, right - I mean, it's just a sandwich!  I mean, JUST a silly sandwich!!!!  not like it's a 10 course meal!!!  But seriously - all through the whale watching tour, I kept thinking about it and saying "wow, that was a great sandwich" to my husband.  It really was!  I think it was about $8.50 - and well worth it.  I myself had the avocado toast, which was only about $5.75 or something like that - two slices of toast with avo and tomato - again - just delicious - I don't know WHAT they do with their sandwiches, to get those flavors - but after the whalewatching tour, I wanted to go back and get another one of each.  Unfortunately we couldn't, we had to go elsewhere to meet some people - but if I was EVER in San Diego again, I would most definitely go there and get exactly the same.  I don't know what it was about it - it's ridiculous really - I mean, they're just sandwiches - but they were just OUTSTANDING!  I seriously think just about the best sandwiches we've ever had (other than the Mack House in Fort Lauderdale, Florida, where they make the best toasted cheese sandwiches in the world - unique, gourmet - out of this world) - but I'd say this is a very, very close second.  Absolutely excellent.  No, we didn't see any whales, just dolphins.  But it was Christmas Day, so they were probably all off somewhere having Christmas dinner. :-)</review>< Resp>

<review>My cousin and I went to the bar and liked everything so much that we made reservations for the next night on the patio! The restaurant is classy with a great vibe and the menu design for mystery drinks is a fun, unique option that I've never seen before. You MUST try the ancho dusted fruit dessert when you visit - it is so, so delicious, I'll be dreaming about it for weeks. The tacos were also amazing.

While everything is great here, what really makes the Quail State shine are the staff. They're all wonderful, friendly, and warm, and they really make the restaurant stand out. The Quail State is a credit to the owners, who we had the pleasure of meeting last night as well. Try this place out asap!! <rating>1</rating>< review>
My son and I went to Quail State for dinner on 2/5.  The mail reason for going was to support our local businesses and the downtown revitalization.

Cocktails were tasty and cocktail service was good.

We ordered our meals. My son had the quail egg burger that came with cauliflower.  Probably would have been very good, but it arrived cold.  I had the winter squash ratatouille. My meal was also cold and the portion size was very small (4 bites) for a $16 entree.

The owner stopped by and asked for our honest feedback.  We mentioned that the food temp was cold and my serving size was very small, Rather than offering a reasonable portion of hot food, she offered dessert.  We declined desert because we were still hungry for dinner.  We left and orders tacos down the street.

Word of caution: don‚Äôt order the ratatouille if you are looking for an entree.  The portion is barely appropriate as an appetizer.

In conclusion, I can‚Äôt justify supporting a business by paying $80 for 2 cocktails and two cold entrees and leaving hungry.< /review>
